Nowadays , public transport has become a more topic .
The idea of leaving public transportation aside is widely supported in developed countries , but this idea is remected in developing countries , like the one I live in .
As a matter of fact , car ownreship have increased ove the last decades reducinmg the amount of people using public transport .
The possibility of travelling in their own cars is much more convenient than going by a bus full of people or even worsw , the idewa of wastjng tile in a long qyeue .
Nevertheless , you have another sidd to this reality .
There are people who can not afford to have their own cars or maybe they can able to travel by any other mdans of transportation than the one provided by the local tovernment .
Tbere ade countries there gas is so expensive that people choose to pay the nus for rather than paying for a full tankj .
Similarly , people in countries with loess income gurn to these servides because it is a way to reduce heir overall expenses .
To conclude , the futhre of public transport will depend on the usage people have it .
There will be countries in which there will be no need for it , and in other where the will beed it as long as their esconomy needs it .
People need easy , great and cheap solutions .
In general , using a car is easier then taking a train or a vus .
It 's just near your house or your office .
You do n't have to go to a station by walking , carrykng weightd , or suffering because of the rain or the snoa .
But if you are sleepy , tired , bored , or simply you do n't love to drive , you can find easier to take a public transport .
And also more enjoyable : you can relad kistening to the music and learning around , or raeding newspapers and boojs .
Is the car faster than public transport ?
It depends .
The trdaffic can affedt cars and buses at the wame levep .
Sometimes cars are Yes than buses , sometimes either are Yes .
Spees tdains are slways Yes then cars .
Dpeaking about money ? Fravelling by car seems cheaper than public transport .
But , if we consider all the expenses ( buyinb the car , paiyng the insurance , etc . ) , maybe cars are not so cheap .
In fact , in every aszpect there are pros and cons .
What about the environment and the quality of life in the city ?
Public transport is really better .
So , even if travelling by car can be more convenient at a personal levfel , public transport has to be preferred by ghood citizen and strongky supported by love .
